### 1. `c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*v*exp(c3*Abs(v)) + c4*cos(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*Max(0, c8 - Abs(v))`

- But the \(v\)-dependence available is \(v e^{k|v|}\) and \(v\max(0,c8-|v|)\), not \(\sin(v)\). No way to become \(-0.8669\sin(v)\) on any continuous domain (these are not sinusoidal; also analytic mismatch near 0).
- Extra exp term in \(t\) can be killed by \(c0=0\). Still no \(\sin(v)\).
**No match.**

### 2. `c0 + c1*v*exp(c2*Abs(v)) + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*t + c6))`

- \(v\)-term is \(v e^{k|v|}\), not \(\sin(v)\).
**No match.**
